***socialisme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:socialisme.html>socialisme</a> (19545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:socialisme.html>socialisme</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sociaal.html>sociaal</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-isme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:socialisme.html>socialisme</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:socialisme.html>socialismes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">socialism</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">left ideology</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***sodomiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sodomiet.html>sodomiet</a> (99645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sodomite</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Sodomite, inhabitant of Sodom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sodomīta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σοδομίτης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sodomítēs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Sodom</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-iet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sodomiet.html>sodomiet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sodomieten.html>sodomieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sodomiet.html>sodomietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sodomite, a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> who penetrates another <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> anally or <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more generally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> any male homosexual.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:soeplepel.html>soeplepel</a> (79485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:soep.html>soep</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lepel.html>lepel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spoon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:soeverein.html>soeverein</a> (33028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">soverein</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">soverain</i>. Influenced in the first vowel by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">souverain</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">souverain</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

***soiree.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:soiree.html>soiree</a> (41541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">soirée</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evening activity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:soiree.html>soiree</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:soirees.html>soirees</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A formal evening party.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sōl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the sun</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-ārium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">of purpose, for the sense of <i>sundial</i>; of place, for the sense of <i>terrace</i></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> *<i>sōlārius</i> (relating to the sun).

***solderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:solderen.html>solderen</a> (79476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">souderen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">souder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">solidō</i>. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:solderen.html>solderen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally Eastern Dutch and began to replace the form <i>souderen</i> starting in the late seventeenth century, which <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> apparently come to be regarded as substandard; this obsolete form existed until the early nineteenth century.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg/220px-Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg/330px-Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg/440px-Adafruit_PiTFT_-_Soldering_%2814675479295%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="2659" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>Iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:solderen.html>solderen</a></b>. — Someone <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>soldering</i>.</div></div></div>

</p>

***sommeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sommeren.html>sommeren</a> (112888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sommer</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sommeren.html>sommeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to sum up, to add up</li>
<li>to demand, to <a href = vnd.unilang:dun.html>dun</a> (a payment)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sommeren.html>sommeren</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> authoriteit <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevel.html>bevel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a>

***sommige.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> (838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sommich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">somich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:som.html>som</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">any, some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ich</i>. The simplex <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:som.html>som</a></i> derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">any, some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sumaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found also in other combinations such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">somtijds</i>.
</p><p>Related to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">some</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>some
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>Sommige</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kippen.html>kippen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ei.html>ei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dooiers.html>dooiers</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Some</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hens.html>hens</a> occasionally lay an egg with two yolks.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
